805	            end_marker = " "
806	
807	            # get hidden states from language model
808	            all_hidden_states_in_lm = self.lm.get_representation(
809	                text_sentences, start_marker, end_marker, self.chars_per_chunk
810	            )

784	
785	    @property
786	    def embedding_length(self) -> int:
787	        return self.__embedding_length
788	
789	    def _add_embeddings_internal(self, sentences: list[Sentence]) -> list[Sentence]:
790	        # gradients are enable if fine-tuning is enabled
791	        gradient_context = torch.enable_grad() if self.fine_tune else torch.no_grad()
792	
793	        with gradient_context:
794	            # if this is not possible, use LM to generate embedding. First, get text sentences
795	            text_sentences = (
796	                [sentence.to_tokenized_string() for sentence in sentences]
797	                if self.tokenized_lm
798	                else [sentence.to_plain_string() for sentence in sentences]
799	            )
800	
801	            if self.is_lower:
802	                text_sentences = [sentence.lower() for sentence in text_sentences]
803	
804	            start_marker = self.lm.document_delimiter if "document_delimiter" in self.lm.__dict__ else "\n"
805	            end_marker = " "
806	
807	            # get hidden states from language model
808	            all_hidden_states_in_lm = self.lm.get_representation(
809	                text_sentences, start_marker, end_marker, self.chars_per_chunk
810	            )
811	
812	            if not self.fine_tune:
813	                all_hidden_states_in_lm = all_hidden_states_in_lm.detach()
814	
815	            # take first or last hidden states from language model as word representation
816	            for i, sentence in enumerate(sentences):
817	                sentence_text = sentence.to_tokenized_string() if self.tokenized_lm else sentence.to_plain_string()
818	
819	                offset_forward: int = len(start_marker)
820	                offset_backward: int = len(sentence_text) + len(start_marker)
821	
822	                for token in sentence.tokens:
823	                    offset_forward += len(token.text)
824	                    if self.is_forward_lm:
825	                        offset_with_whitespace = offset_forward
826	                        offset_without_whitespace = offset_forward - 1
827	                    else:
828	                        offset_with_whitespace = offset_backward
829	                        offset_without_whitespace = offset_backward - 1
830	
831	                    # offset mode that extracts at whitespace after last character
832	                    if self.with_whitespace:
833	                        embedding = all_hidden_states_in_lm[offset_with_whitespace, i, :]
834	                    # offset mode that extracts at last character
835	                    else:
836	                        embedding = all_hidden_states_in_lm[offset_without_whitespace, i, :]
837	
838	                    if self.tokenized_lm or token.whitespace_after > 0:
839	                        offset_forward += 1
840	                        offset_backward -= 1
841	
842	                    offset_backward -= len(token.text)
843	
844	                    token.set_embedding(self.name, embedding)
845	
846	            del all_hidden_states_in_lm
847	
848	        return sentences
849	
850	    def __str__(self) -> str:
851	        return self.name
852	
853	    def to_params(self):
854	        return {
855	            "fine_tune": self.fine_tune,
856	            "chars_per_chunk": self.chars_per_chunk,
857	            "is_lower": self.is_lower,
858	            "tokenized_lm": self.tokenized_lm,
859	            "model_params": {
860	                "dictionary": self.lm.dictionary,
861	                "is_forward_lm": self.lm.is_forward_lm,
862	                "hidden_size": self.lm.hidden_size,
863	                "nlayers": self.lm.nlayers,
864	                "embedding_size": self.lm.embedding_size,

788	
789	    def _add_embeddings_internal(self, sentences: list[Sentence]) -> list[Sentence]:
790	        # gradients are enable if fine-tuning is enabled
791	        gradient_context = torch.enable_grad() if self.fine_tune else torch.no_grad()
792	
793	        with gradient_context:
794	            # if this is not possible, use LM to generate embedding. First, get text sentences
795	            text_sentences = (
796	                [sentence.to_tokenized_string() for sentence in sentences]
797	                if self.tokenized_lm
798	                else [sentence.to_plain_string() for sentence in sentences]
799	            )
800	
801	            if self.is_lower:
802	                text_sentences = [sentence.lower() for sentence in text_sentences]
803	
804	            start_marker = self.lm.document_delimiter if "document_delimiter" in self.lm.__dict__ else "\n"
805	            end_marker = " "
806	
807	            # get hidden states from language model
808	            all_hidden_states_in_lm = self.lm.get_representation(
809	                text_sentences, start_marker, end_marker, self.chars_per_chunk
810	            )
811	
812	            if not self.fine_tune:
813	                all_hidden_states_in_lm = all_hidden_states_in_lm.detach()
814	
815	            # take first or last hidden states from language model as word representation
816	            for i, sentence in enumerate(sentences):
817	                sentence_text = sentence.to_tokenized_string() if self.tokenized_lm else sentence.to_plain_string()
818	
819	                offset_forward: int = len(start_marker)
820	                offset_backward: int = len(sentence_text) + len(start_marker)
821	
822	                for token in sentence.tokens:
823	                    offset_forward += len(token.text)
824	                    if self.is_forward_lm:
825	                        offset_with_whitespace = offset_forward
826	                        offset_without_whitespace = offset_forward - 1
827	                    else:
828	                        offset_with_whitespace = offset_backward
829	                        offset_without_whitespace = offset_backward - 1
830	
831	                    # offset mode that extracts at whitespace after last character
832	                    if self.with_whitespace:
833	                        embedding = all_hidden_states_in_lm[offset_with_whitespace, i, :]
834	                    # offset mode that extracts at last character
835	                    else:
836	                        embedding = all_hidden_states_in_lm[offset_without_whitespace, i, :]
837	
838	                    if self.tokenized_lm or token.whitespace_after > 0:
839	                        offset_forward += 1
840	                        offset_backward -= 1
841	
842	                    offset_backward -= len(token.text)
843	
844	                    token.set_embedding(self.name, embedding)
845	
846	            del all_hidden_states_in_lm
847	
848	        return sentences
849	
850	    def __str__(self) -> str:
851	        return self.name
852	
853	    def to_params(self):
854	        return {
855	            "fine_tune": self.fine_tune,
856	            "chars_per_chunk": self.chars_per_chunk,
857	            "is_lower": self.is_lower,
858	            "tokenized_lm": self.tokenized_lm,
859	            "model_params": {
860	                "dictionary": self.lm.dictionary,
861	                "is_forward_lm": self.lm.is_forward_lm,
862	                "hidden_size": self.lm.hidden_size,
863	                "nlayers": self.lm.nlayers,
864	                "embedding_size": self.lm.embedding_size,
865	                "nout": self.lm.nout,
